Hypotheses tested: (H1) real momentum pressure-force oscillation rejected after CHK-029 because T=2.5 face pressure acceleration remains O(`1e-2`) and KE never reaches `1e-3`; (H2) bulk phase pressure oscillation rejected: T=2.5 liquid bulk RMS residual `1.409e-02`, gas bulk RMS residual `1.673e-04`, pressure contrast stays `0.1677..0.2908`; (H3) checkerboard/PPE mode rejected: checker projection `1.953e-02`; (H4) raw nodal scalar is nonphysical in the diffuse interface band supported: `99.87%` of gauge-free pressure residual energy is in `0.05<œà<0.95`, concentrated near `0.45<œà<0.55`, while bulk and face cochain are stable; (H5) visualization contract error supported by sharp-interface theory: affine-jump IPC defines physical pressure work in `A_f(G_f p-B_f(j))`, and scalar pressure is single-valued only in each phase with a jump on Œì. Fix: added output-only `pressure_bulk` snapshot renderer that masks the undefined diffuse interface layer (no smoothing/capping/damping) and updated N64 alpha-2 configs to use `pressure_bulk_t*.pdf`; raw scalar remains stored in `fields/pressure` for diagnostics. | session_CHK | CHK-RA-OSC-N64-029 DONE 2026-05-05 ‚Äî User observation„ÄåÂúßÂäõ„ÅåÁïåÈù¢‰ªòËøë„ÅßÂ§â„Å™ÊåØÂãï„ÄçÂØæÂøú„ÄÇRCA: affine pressure-jump IPC was solving with a previous face-pressure history in the predictor but then reusing the new full affine jump cochain as the velocity correction and next history; this violates the split PPE unknown/jump contract (`œá=Œ¥p` needs `Œ¥j`, or full-pressure solve needs source `D_f a_p^n` and correction `a_p^{n+1}-a_p^n`). Fix: keep the mathematically full face pressure cochain as history, add `D_f a_p^n` to the affine PPE source, apply only the cochain increment in the corrector, and store `a_p^{n+1}` for the next predictor. | session_CHK | CHK-RA-CH9-AFFINE-GAUGE-001 DONE 2026-04-30 ‚Äî User ÊåáÁ§∫„Äåaffine„ÅÆÊÝ∏ÂøÉÊù°‰ª∂„ÄéÊó¢Áü•„Ç∏„É£„É≥„Éó„ÇíÊ∫Ä„Åü„ÅôÂúßÂäõ„Å™„Çâ cut-face flux „ÅåÊ∂à„Åà„Çã„Äè„ÅåÂ£ä„Çå„ÇãÁêÜÁî±„ÇíÁêÜË´ñÁöÑ„Å´Ë£è‰ªò„Åë„Åó„Å¶„ÄÇ„Åù„Çå„Çí„ÇÇ„Å£„Å¶„ÄÅË´ñÊñá„Åã„ÇâÂâäÈô§„Åó„Åü„ÅÑ„ÄçÂØæÂøú„ÄÇTheory: affine cut-face flux is one coupled face operator `F_{\Gamma,f}=\alpha_f(G_f(p)-B_f(j_\Gamma))`; the known-jump zero-flux invariant requires the same nonzero cut-face coefficient to multiply both the pressure-gradient part and the jump lifting. A detached phase-block / per-phase Neumann gauge sets the cross-phase pressure coefficient to zero; if the known-jump coefficient remains nonzero, a pressure satisfying the jump still leaves residual cut-face flux, while setting it to zero removes the capillary drive itself. Therefore production affine has one global null mode and uses a fixed global gauge/pin, not phase-mean gauge. Paper: `paper/sections/09b_split_ppe.tex`, `paper/sections/09e_ppe_bc.tex`, `paper/sections/09f_pressure_summary.tex` updated to remove production endorsement of phase-mean gauge and document the invariant failure. Validation: `git diff --check` PASS; `latexmk -xelatex -interaction=nonstopmode -halt-on-error main.tex` PASS (`paper/main.pdf`, 234 pp). [SOLID-X] paper-only; no production code change. |

Added controls `sigma0`, `g0`, `noforce`, `alpha1`; remote GPU showed alpha=2 baseline / sigma0 / g0 all BLOWUP near `t‚âà0.007`, no-force alpha=2 exactly static to `T=0.02`, alpha=1 stable to `T=0.02`. Identified non-uniform-grid projection closure mismatch: FVM PPE solves face harmonic `rho_face` operator, corrector applies nodal `rho_i^{-1}` averaged gradient, so `D_FVM M^{-1}G != A_FVM`. Added partial PoC [gradient_operator.py](../src/twophase/simulation/gradient_operator.py) `FVMDivergenceOperator` / `CCDDivergenceOperator` and [ns_pipeline.py](../src/twophase/simulation/ns_pipeline.py) paired divergence for PPE RHS + debug divergence; targeted local `test_ns_pipeline_fccd.py` 6 passed. Remote GPU PoC reduced max residual but still BLOWUP, confirming RHS-only fix is insufficient. Production remedy: face-flux projection/corrector + conservative face-to-node reconstruction. Report: [docs/memo/ch13_05_rising_bubble_root_cause_hypotheses.md](memo/ch13_05_rising_bubble_root_cause_hypotheses.md). Branch: worktree-rising-bubble |

# ¬ß LESSONS (KL-01..12)

## ¬ßA ‚Äî Known Error Classes (Math/Code)

| KL | Failure | Fix Pattern |
|---|---|---|
| KL-01 | Block matrix (2,1) sign flip after RHS transposition | Read RHS coeff ‚Üí negate ‚Üí write to LHS |
| KL-02 | Wrong block size (3√ó3 vs 2√ó2) in docs | Verify block dims against actual code arrays |
| KL-03 | Pseudocode comment names wrong algorithm | Cross-check comment vs accumulation pattern |
| KL-04 | D(Œ∫f) ‚âÝ Œ∫D(f) for varying Œ∫ | Expand D(Œ∫f); never factor variable coefficients |
| KL-05 | Nyquist modified wavenumber ‚âÝ finite-grid spectral radius | Compute spectral radius of actual discrete matrix |
| KL-06 | Pre-asymptotic O(h‚Å¥) mistaken for asymptotic | Confirm slope stability over ‚â•3 grid doublings |
| KL-07 | "Conservative" CFL rounding wrong direction | Smaller dt: floor dt, ceiling Nsteps |
| KL-08 | Kronecker C-order vs Fortran-order confusion | State convention explicitly; verify with N=2 example |
| KL-09 | PPE LGMRES-primary/LU-fallback vs LU-primary confusion | LGMRES primary; spsolve auto-fallback on non-convergence (pre-2026-04-15) |
| KL-10 | Collocated corrector "exact CCD-div-free" claim | RC PPE gives ‚Äñ‚àá_RC¬∑u^{n+1}‚Äñ=0; CCD residual remains O(h¬≤) |
| KL-11 | Pin-node excl still targets (0,0) after move to center | Use `pin_dof = ravel_multi_index(tuple(n//2 for n in grid.N), grid.shape)` |
| KL-12 | `\texorpdfstring` missing in math heading ‚Üí xelatex infinite loop | Wrap numbered math headings; pre-compile grep required |
